‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§ø‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡•ã‡§§‡•ç‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§§‡•á ‡§è‡§∑ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡•ã ‡§ú‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§§‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡•ã‡§Æ‡•á ‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§ø‡§É ‡•´‡•™) ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§Ω‡§®‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ ‡•§ ‡§ï‡•ç‡§µ ‡§™‡•Å‡§®‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§É ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§Ω‡§µ‡§Ø‡§µ‡§æ ‡§ã‡§ó‡§æ‡§¶‡§Ø‡§É 2 ‡§§‡•á ‡§ö ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∂‡§¨‡•ç‡§¶‡§æ‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡•á‡§¶‡§Ø‡§Ç‡§§‡•á ‡§Æ‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ï‡§æ ‡§è‡§µ ‡§ã‡§ó‡§æ‡§¶‡§Ø ‡§á‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§ö‡§æ ‡§á‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•É‡§ö‡§æ‡§Æ‡§™‡§ø ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ï‡§Ç ‡§è‡§µ‡§û‡•ç‡§ö ‡§∏‡§æ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§ø ‡§ö‡•á‡§®‡•ç‡§¶‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§á‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ß‡§ø‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡§Æ‡•Å‡§™‡§∞‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡§æ‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§‡§ø ‡•§ ‡§á‡§¶‡§Æ‡•ç ‘‡§Ö‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§®‡•ç‡§ß‡§É ‡•§ (‡§µ‡§æ‡§£‡§ó ‡§∏‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ ‡§á‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ï‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§ø‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§ï‡§æ‡§Æ‡§®‡§É) ‡§∏‡§æ‡§π‡§ö‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç ‡§∂‡§¨‡•ç‡§¶‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§Æ‡§ø‡§ï‡§æ‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Æ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ç ‡§π‡•ç‡§Ø‡§∞‡•ç‡§ö‡§§‡•Ä‡§§‡§ø ‡§™‡•É‡§•‡§ø‡§µ‡•Ä‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡•á‡§® ‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•Ç‡§Ø‡§§‡•á ‡•§ ‡§® ‡§ö ‡§§‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡•ã ‡§Ω‡§Ø‡§Ç Eggeling
  1. Threefold, forsooth, is science; the RÃ•cs, the Yajus, and the SƒÅmans. The RÃ•cs are this (earth), since it is thereon that he who sings them, does sing them; the RÃ•cs are speech, since it is by speech that he who sings them, does sing them. And the Yajus, forsooth, are the air, and the SƒÅmans the sky. That same threefold science is used in the Soma-sacrifice.

Eggeling
  1. By the RÃ•c he conquers this world, by the Yajus the air, and by the SƒÅman the sky. Therefore whosoever has learnt one of these sciences, let him endeavour to learn also what is contained in the two others: by the RÃ•c, forsooth, he conquers this world, by the Yajus the air, and by the SƒÅman the sky.

Therefore in the Sadas they perform (the ≈öastras and Stotras) with the RÃ•c and SƒÅman, for the Sadas is Indra’s own.

  1. And by means of these Yajus they, as it were, bring forward (puras) that Vish·πáu, the sacrifice: hence the name ‘pura≈õcara·πáa’ (preparatory ceremony).

Eggeling
  1. Both the RÃ•cs and the SƒÅmans are Speech, and the Yajus are the Mind. Now wherever this Speech was, there everything was done, everything was known; but wherever Mind was, there nothing whatever was done, nothing was known, for no one knows (understands) those who think in their mind.

Eggeling
  1. The gods said to Speech, ‘Go thou forward and make this known!’ She said, ‘What will be my reward then?’–‘Whatever in the sacrifice is offered with SvƒÅhƒÅ, and without Vasha·π≠, that shall be thine!’ Hence whatever in the sacrifice is offered with SvƒÅhƒÅ, and without Vasha·π≠, that belongs to Speech. She then went forward and made that known, saying, ‘Do this so! do this so!’

‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ø‡§£‡§É

[‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§®‡§Ç ‡§∏‡§™‡•ç‡§§‡§Æ‡•á]

Eggeling
  1. And hence they also perform with the Yajus in the Sadas: they raise up the Udumbara post, they erect the Sadas, they throw up the dhish·πáya hearths,–for thus they became yoke-fellows.

‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§∂‡§®‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡§Æ‡•á‡§µ ‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∞‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•É‡§§‡§Æ‡•ç ‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§¶‡§ø ‡§ö ‡§§‡•á‡§®‡§æ‡§™‡§ø ‡§¶‡•É‡§∂‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡•á ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡§É ‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§§‡•ã ‡§® ‡§§‡§¶‡•ç‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡•à‡§∞‡•Å‡§™‡§æ‡§Ø‡§É ‡§ï‡§∞‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§¶‡§∞‡•ç‡§∂‡§®‡•ã‡§™‡§æ‡§Ø‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§µ‡§∏‡•ç‡§•‡§Ø‡§æ‡§™‡§ø ‡§ö ‡§¶‡•ã‡§∑‡•ã ‡§Ω‡§µ‡§§‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§†‡§§‡•á ‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§•‡§æ ‡§§‡§¶‡•á‡§µ ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§•‡•Å‡§®‡§Ç ‡§≤‡•ã‡§ï‡•á ‡§ö‡§æ‡§®‡•Å‡§Æ‡§æ‡§®‡§ø‡§ï‡§Ç ‡§§‡§Æ‡§™‡§ø ‡§≤‡§ú‡•ç‡§ú‡§Ø‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡§ø ‡§ï‡§ø‡§Ç ‡§§‡§∞‡•ç‡§π‡§ø ‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§Æ‡•á‡§µ ‡•• ‡•Ø ‡••

Eggeling
  1. That same Sadas they enclose on all sides with a view to that generation, thinking, ‘Quite secretly shall be carried on that generation!’ for improper, indeed, is the generation which another sees hence even when a husband and wife are seen, while carrying on intercourse, they run away from each other, for they give offence. Therefore to any one looking into the Sadas, except through the door, let him say, ‘Look not!’ for it is as if he were seeing intercourse being carried on. Freely (one may look) through the door, for the door is made by the gods.

‡•ß‡•¶

‡§µ‡§ø‡§∂‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§∏-‡§™‡•ç‡§∞‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•Å‡§§‡§ø‡§É

‡§∏‡§æ‡§Ø‡§£‡§É

‡§è‡§µ‡§Æ‡•á‡§µ‡•à‡§§‡§¶‡§ø‡§§‡§ø ‡•§ ‡§™‡•Ç‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ‡§Æ‡•á‡§∑‡§æ ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§ñ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§§‡§æ ‡•• ‡•ß‡•¶ ‡••

Eggeling
  1. In like manner they enclose the HavirdhƒÅna on all sides with a view to that generation, thinking, ‘Quite secretly this generation shall be carried on!’ for improper, indeed, is the generation which another sees: hence even when a husband and wife are seen, while carrying on intercourse, they run away from each other, for they give offence. Therefore to any one looking into the HavirdhƒÅna, except through the door, let him say, ‘Look not!’ for it is as if he were seeing intercourse being carried on. Freely (one may look) through the door, for the door is made by the gods.

Eggeling
  1. And there, in the HavirdhƒÅna, that male, the Soma, longs after the female, the water. From that generation the moon was produced: from food, indeed, food is produced, viz. the moon from water and Soma; for the moon is the food of him that burns yonder 8. Hence he thereby produces the sacrificer, and for him he produces food: from the RÃ•c and SƒÅman he produces the sacrificer, and from water and Soma he produces food for him.

Eggeling
  1. They performed with them in a low voice, and thereby strengthened them; and henceforth that science was equal to the other two sciences, and the air-world was equal to the two other worlds. Therefore the Yajus, while being distinct, are yet indistinct; and therefore the air-world, while being distinct, is yet indistinct (indefinable).

Eggeling
  1. He who performs with the Yajus in a low voice, strengthens them; and they, thus strengthened, strengthen him. But he who performs in a loud voice, weakens them, and, being weak, they weaken him.

Eggeling
  1. The RÃ•cs and SƒÅmans, forsooth, are speech, and the Yajus are the mind; and so those who perform with the RÃ•c and SƒÅman are speech, and those who perform with the Yajus are the mind. Hence nothing whatever is done, unless ordered by the Adhvaryu: when the Adhvaryu says, ‘Recite (the invitatory prayer)! Pronounce the offering prayer!’ then those who perform with the RÃ•k perform it. And when the Adhvaryu says, ‘Soma becometh pure: turn ye back 10!’ then those who perform with the SƒÅman perform it,–for speech speaks not but what is conceived by the mind.

Eggeling
  1. Thus, then, the Adhvaryu, the mind, walks, as it were, in front (pura≈õ-carati): hence the name ‘pura≈õcara·πáa 11;’ and verily, he who knows this, stands, as it were, in front through prosperity and glory.

‡§§‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ ‡§è‡§§‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡•á‡§§‡§ø ‡•§ ‡§Ö‡§µ‡•à‡§¶‡§ø‡§ï‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§∞‡§£‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø ‘‡§Ü‡§µ‡•É‡§§‡§æ’ ‡§Ö‡§ß‡•ç‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Å‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§∞‡•á‡§¶‡•ç ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§π‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§π‡§£‡§æ‡§¶‡•á‡§§‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•Å‡§ö‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§‡•á, ‡§∏‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•ã‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§∂‡§∏‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•á ‡§ö‡§æ‡§ó‡•ç‡§∞‡§π‡•á‡§∑‡•ç‡§µ‡•á‡§µ ‡§§‡§¶‡§æ‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§®‡§Ç ‡§¶‡•ç‡§∞‡§∑‡•ç‡§ü‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§Ç, ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§∞‡§£‡§∏‡§Ç‡§¨‡§®‡•ç‡§ß‡§µ‡§ø‡§ß‡§æ‡§®‡§æ‡§§‡•ç ‡•§ ‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§∞ ‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ (?) ‡§®‡§∞‡§æ‡§™‡•á‡§ï‡•ç‡§∑‡§Ø‡§æ ‡§™‡•Å‡§∞‡§∂‡•ç‡§ö‡§∞‡§£‡§∏‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§§‡•ç‡§™‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•á‡§É ‘‡§∏ ‡§Ø‡•ã ‡§π‡•à‡§µ‡§Ç ‡§µ‡§ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§®‡•ç’ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§∂‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§Æ‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡•á ‡§Ω‡§ß‡•ç‡§µ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ã‡§É ‡§´‡§≤‡§Æ‡•ç ‡•• ‡•®‡•ß ‡••

‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§∂‡•ç‡§∞‡•Ä‡§Æ‡§¶‡§æ‡§ö‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§Ø‡§π‡§∞‡§ø‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ‡§Æ‡§ø‡§®‡§É ‡§ï‡•É‡§§‡•å ‡§Æ‡§æ‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§®‡•ç‡§¶‡§ø‡§®‡§∂‡§§‡§™‡§•‡§¨‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§π‡•ç‡§Æ‡§£‡§≠‡§æ‡§∑‡•ç‡§Ø‡•á ‡§ö‡§§‡•Å‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡§ï‡§æ‡§£‡•ç‡§°‡•á ‡§∑‡§∑‡•ç‡§†‡•á ‡§Ω‡§ß‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ø‡•á ‡§∏‡§™‡•ç‡§§‡§Æ‡§Ç ‡§¨‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§π‡•ç‡§Æ‡§£‡§Æ‡•ç ‡•• ‡•™-‡•¨-‡•≠ ‡••

Eggeling
  1. Now that same pura≈õcara·πáa (going before) is nothing else than yonder burning (sun): one ought to perform in accordance with his (the sun’s) course. When he (the Adhvaryu) has drawn a cup of Soma, let him turn round in accordance with his course; when he has responded (to the HotrÃ•’s recitation), let him turn round in accordance with his course; when he has offered a graha, let him turn round in accordance with his course: he (the sun), verily, is the supporter; and whosoever, knowing this, is able to perform in accordance with his course, he, forsooth, is able to support his dependants 13.
